<content>
1: # pge-jax — Agent Instructions
2: 
3: ## Project Structure
4: 
5: ```
6: pge-jax/
7: ├── pge_jax/          # Package source
8: │   ├── __init__.py   # Public API — add new exports here
9: │   ├── model.py      # JAXModel: sympy → JAX evaluation wrapper
10: │   ├── optimize.py   # LM and BFGS optimizers
11: │   ├── metrics.py    # JAX-native regression metrics
12: │   └── evaluate.py   # High-level fit/predict/evaluate pipeline
13: ├── tests/            # pytest test suite
14: ├── pyproject.toml    # Build config, deps, tool settings
15: ├── README.md         # User-facing documentation
16: └── AGENTS.md         # This file
17: ```
18: 
19: ## Running the Code
20: 
21: ```bash
22: # Enter the venv (created during setup)
23: source .venv/bin/activate
24: 
25: # Run all tests
26: python -m pytest tests/ -v
27: 
28: # Run a single test file
29: python -m pytest tests/test_model.py -v
30: 
31: # Run a single test
32: python -m pytest tests/test_model.py::TestJAXModel::test_linear_model_basic -v
33: 
34: # Lint
35: ruff check pge_jax/ tests/
36: 
37: # Format
38: ruff format pge_jax/ tests/
39: 
40: # Type check
41: mypy pge_jax/
42: ```
43: 
44: ## Coding Conventions
45: 
46: - **Python 3.11+** — use modern syntax: `X | Y` unions, `match`/`case`, `typing.Self`
47: - **120-char line limit** — configured in `pyproject.toml`
48: - **Docstrings** — Google style (parameters, returns, raises sections)
49: - **Imports** — standard library first, then third-party, then local (`pge_jax.*`), alphabetized within groups
50: - **No bare `import jax`** — always `import jax.numpy as jnp` for array ops
51: - **Type hints** — preferred on all public functions and class attributes
52: - **No print statements** in library code — use logging or return values
53: 
54: ## Core Architecture
55: 
56: ### The Evaluation Pipeline
57: 
58: The key abstraction is `JAXModel` (model.py). It wraps a sympy expression and provides JAX-compatible evaluation:
59: 
60: 1. **Symbol extraction** — `_extract_coeffs_and_vars()` splits `expr.free_symbols` into coefficients (`C_*`) and variables. Sorted by string name for determinism.
61: 
62: 2. **JAX function construction** — `sympy.lambdify(all_syms, expr, modules="jax")` creates a callable. The wrapper unpacks the coefficient array into individual args matching the lambdify signature.
63: 
64: 3. **Jacobian** — computed via `jax.jacfwd` + `jax.vmap`. Each sample's Jacobian is computed independently and batched.
65: 
66: 4. **Optimization** — `fit_levenberg_marquardt()` in optimize.py solves the damped normal equations. The Jacobian from step 3 feeds directly into the LM step.
67: 
68: ### Data Flow
69: 
70: ```
71: sympy.Expr → JAXModel.__init__() → jax_fun, jac_fun
72:                                 → fit_levenberg_marquardt()
73:                                 → FitResult(coefficients, predictions, cost, ...)
74: ```
75: 
76: ### Key Types
77: 
78: ```python
79: @dataclass
80: class FitResult:
81:     success: bool
82:     coefficients: jnp.ndarray   # optimized coefficients
83:     predictions: jnp.ndarray    # model predictions at optimized coeffs
84:     cost: float                 # sum of squared residuals
85:     n_residuals: int
86:     n_params: int
87:     message: str = ""
88:     nfev: int = 0
89: 
90: @dataclass
91: class EvalResult:
92:     fit: FitResult
93:     score: float        # RMSE
94:     r2: float
95:     evar: float
96:     aic: float
97:     bic: float
98:     chisqr: float
99:     redchi: float
100:     mae: float
101:     rmae: float
102:     predictions: jnp.ndarray
103: ```
104: 
105: ## Gotchas
106: 
107: ### JAX float64
108: 
109: JAX defaults to float32 on most platforms. To use float64 you need:
110: 
111: ```python
112: jax.config.update("jax_enable_x64", True)
113: ```
114: 
115: Or set the env var: `JAX_ENABLE_X64=1`. The current code requests float64 in `jnp.asarray(..., dtype=jnp.float64)` which triggers warnings when x64 is disabled. Tests pass with float32, but precision-sensitive work (e.g., symbolic regression convergence) may need x64.
116: 
117: ### sympy.lambdify + JAX
118: 
119: - `sympy.lambdify` with `modules="jax"` works for most expressions but falls back to numpy on failure.
120: - Each coefficient symbol becomes a separate argument. The wrapper in `JAXModel.jax_fun` unpacks the coefficient array to match.
121: - If the expression has no variables (constant), `jax_fun` receives no input arrays — handle this case.
122: 
123: ### LM Optimizer Convergence
124: 
125: The LM implementation has multiple convergence criteria:
126: 1. Cost below tolerance (`cost < tol`)
127: 2. Relative cost change below tolerance
128: 3. Coefficient change below tolerance
129: 4. Damping blowup (`mu > 1e12`) — failure
130: 
131: The default `tol=1e-4` works for most cases. The float32 precision means you won't get better than ~1e-6 accuracy regardless.
132: 
133: ### Coefficient Symbol Convention
134: 
135: Coefficients are identified by name prefix: `C_` or `C[`. The original pypge used bare `C` with `rewrite_coeff()` to generate `C_0`, `C_1`, etc. The JAX port assumes this convention is already applied. If you create expressions with bare `C` symbols, they won't be extracted as coefficients.
136: 
137: ### Test Precision
138: 
139: Tests use `atol=5e-3` or `rel=5e-3` tolerances because float32 limits precision. Don't tighten these without first ensuring x64 is enabled.
140: 
141: ## Adding New Code
142: 
143: ### New Metric
144: 
145: 1. Add function to `pge_jax/metrics.py` with Google-style docstring
146: 2. Add import and export in `pge_jax/__init__.py`
147: 3. Add to `EvalResult` in `pge_jax/evaluate.py` if it should be part of the full evaluation
148: 4. Add tests in `tests/test_metrics.py`
149: 
150: ### New Optimizer
151: 
152: 1. Add function to `pge_jax/optimize.py` — return `FitResult`
153: 2. Add import in `pge_jax/__init__.py`
154: 3. Wire into `fit_model()` in `pge_jax/evaluate.py` if it should be a first-class option
155: 4. Add tests in `tests/test_optimize.py`
156: 
157: ### New Model Feature
158: 
159: 1. Modify `JAXModel` in `pge_jax/model.py`
160: 2. Update `_build_jax_functions()` if the change affects evaluation
161: 3. Add tests in `tests/test_model.py`
162: 
163: ## Current Task: Port the Full PGE Search Loop
164: 
165: The evaluation back-end (`JAXModel`, `fit_model`, `evaluate`, metrics) is complete and tested. The next phase is porting the PGE search loop from `pypge/pypge/` to `pge_jax/`.
166: 
167: ### Porting Strategy
168: 
169: - **No DEAP dependency** — fitness values stored as tuples on model objects
170: - **No multiprocessing** — JAX/XLA handles parallelism; skip `parallel.py` initially
171: - **No remote evaluation** — all computation is local via JAX
172: - **No `lmfit` / `sklearn`** — already replaced by JAX-native equivalents
173: - **Model class** — needs a search-loop-aware model with state flags and size metrics, separate from `JAXModel` (which is the pure evaluation wrapper)
174: 
175: ### Porting Order
176: 
177: 1. **`filters.py`** — Expression validity filters (no deps)
178: 2. **`algebra.py`** — Symbolic expand/factor/simplify (only sympy dep)
179: 3. **`memoize.py`** — Hash-based expression deduplication
180: 4. **`fitness_funcs.py`** — Multi-objective fitness construction (no DEAP)
181: 5. **`selection.py`** — NSGA-II / SPEA-II / log-ND sort (standalone)
182: 6. **`expand.py`** — `Grower` class (depends on filters for `_uniquify`)
183: 7. **Search-loop `Model` class** — State tracking, size metrics, parent/child tracking
184: 8. **`search.py`** — `PGE` class orchestrating the full loop
185: 
186: ### Key Adaptations from pypge
187: 
188: - `pypge/Model.params` (lmfit.Parameters) → `jnp.ndarray` coefficients
189: - `pypge/Model.score` (from sklearn) → `EvalResult.score` (from JAX metrics)
190: - `pypge/fit()` (lmfit LM) → `fit_model()` (JAX-native LM via `fit_levenberg_marquardt`)
191: - Fitness objects: replace `FitnessCalculator` DEAP class with simple tuple storage on model objects
192: - `sortLogNondominated` expects `fitness.wvalues` — adapt to use a `wvalues` attribute or property on model objects
193: - `assignCrowdingDist` expects `fitness.crowding_dist` — store as direct attribute on model objects
194: 
195: ## Reference: pypge (Local)
196: 
197: The original implementation is at `pypge/pypge/`. Key modules and their port targets:
198: 
199: | pypge module | pge_jax target | Status |
200: |---|---|---|
201: | `pypge/model.py` (Model class) | Already replaced by `JAXModel` | Done |
202: | `pypge/evaluate.py` (Fit/Eval/Score) | `pge_jax/evaluate.py` + `optimize.py` | Done |
203: | `pypge/fitness_funcs.py` (multi-obj fitness) | `pge_jax/fitness_funcs.py` | **Not ported** |
204: | `pypge/filters.py` (expression filters) | `pge_jax/filters.py` | **Not ported** |
205: | `pypge/algebra.py` (expand/factor/simplify) | `pge_jax/algebra.py` | **Not ported** |
206: | `pypge/memoize.py` (deduplication) | `pge_jax/memoize.py` | **Not ported** |
207: | `pypge/expand.py` (Grower class) | `pge_jax/expand.py` | **Not ported** |
208: | `pypge/selection.py` (NSGA-II, SPEA-II) | `pge_jax/selection.py` | **Not ported** |
209: | `pypge/search.py` (PGE class, main loop) | `pge_jax/search.py` | **Not ported** |
210: | `pypge/parallel.py` (multiprocessing) | `pge_jax/parallel.py` | **Not ported** |
211: | `pypge/base.py` / `creator.py` (DEAP fitness) | `pge_jax/base.py` or inline | **Not ported** |
212: 
213: ---
214: 
215: ## PGE Search Loop — Architecture Reference
216: 
217: ### The Full Search Pipeline
218: 
219: ```
220:                     ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
221:                     │              PGE.fit(X, Y)                   │
222:                     │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────┐  │
223:                     │  │           PRELOOP                      │  │
224:                     │  │ 1. Generate first_exprs()              │  │
225:                     │  │ 2. Filter (remove invalid)             │  │
226:                     │  │ 3. Memoize (deduplicate)               │  │
227:                     │  │ 4. Algebra (expand/factor)             │  │
228:                     │  │ 5. Filter + Memoize again              │  │
229:                     │  │ 6. Peek-evaluate OR full-evaluate      │  │
230:                     │  │ 7. Push to nsga2_list (population)     │  │
231:                     │  │ 8. Push to final (fully evaluated)     │  │
232:                     │  └───────────────────────────────────────┘  │
233:                     │                                              │
234:                     │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────┐  │
235:                     │  │           MAIN LOOP (N iterations)     │  │
236:                     │  │                                       │  │
237:                     │  │  For each expander:                   │  │
238:                     │  │    1. heap_pop() — NSGA-II select     │  │
239:                     │  │    2. grower.grow() — expand models   │  │
240:                     │  │                                       │  │
241:                     │  │ 3. Filter expanded models             │  │
242:                     │  │ 4. Memoize (deduplicate)              │  │
243:                     │  │ 5. Algebra (expand/factor)            │  │
244:                     │  │ 6. Filter + Memoize again             │  │
245:                     │  │                                       │  │
246:                     │  │ 7. Peek-evaluate unique models        │  │
247:                     │  │ 8. Push to nsga2_peek heap            │  │
248:                     │  │ 9. heap_pop(nsga2_peek)               │  │
249:                     │  │ 10. Full-evaluate selected models     │  │
250:                     │  │ 11. Push to final                     │  │
251:                     │  │ 12. Push to nsga2_list                │  │
252:                     │  └───────────────────────────────────────┘  │
253:                     │                                              │
254:                     │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────┐  │
255:                     │  │          FINALIZE                      │  │
256:                     │  │ 1. Combine final + nsga2_list         │  │
257:                     │  │ 2. sortLogNondominated()              │  │
258:                     │  │ 3. Print Pareto fronts                │  │
259:                     │  │ 4. Stop workers                       │  │
260:                     │  └───────────────────────────────────────┘  │
261:                     └─────────────────────────────────────────────┘
262: ```
263: 
264: ### Component Breakdown
265: 
266: #### 1. Expression Model (`pypge/model.py`)
267: 
268: The `Model` class wraps a sympy expression and manages its lifecycle state. Key attributes:
269: 
270: - **Identification**: `id`, `iter_id`, `parent_id`, `gen_relation` (e.g., "first_gen", "var_xpnd", "add_xpnd", "mul_xpnd", "shrunk")
271: - **Expression**: `orig` (original before coeff rewriting), `expr` (expanded after `rewrite_coeff()`), `pretty` (cached string)
272: - **Variables/Coefficients**: `xs` (input variables), `cs` (coefficient symbols `C_0, C_1, ...`), `params` (fitted values)
273: - **Size metrics**: `sz` (tree size), `psz` (penalized size, +2 per function node), `jsz`/`jpsz` (Jacobian sizes), `ncs` (num coefficients)
274: - **Fitness**: `peek_*` (partial fitness on subset), full `score`, `r2`, `evar`, `aic`, `bic`, `chisqr`, `redchi`, `mae`, `rmae`
275: - **Improvement over parent**: `improve_score`, `improve_r2`, etc.
276: - **State flags**: `inited`, `memoized`, `algebrad`, `peeked`, `peek_queued`, `peek_popped`, `evaluated`, `popped`, `expanded`, `finalized`, `errored`
277: 
278: Key method: `rewrite_coeff()` — converts bare `sympy.Symbol('C')` leaves into `C_0, C_1, ...` and creates `lmfit.Parameters`. The JAX port's `JAXModel._extract_coeffs_and_vars()` already handles this.
279: 
280: **Size calculation** (`calc_tree_size`): walks `sympy.preorder_traversal`, counts nodes (+2 penalty per `is_Function`), sums integer absolute values as size.
281: 
282: #### 2. Expression Expansion / Grower (`pypge/expand.py`)
283: 
284: The `Grower` class implements grammar-based expression enumeration. Pre-computed expression pools built in `__init__`:
285: 
286: - **Variable powers**: `xs_pow1` through `xs_pow4` — `x^n`, `x^-n` for n=1..4
287: - **Variable products**: `wout_c_xs1_muls` through `wout_c_xs4_muls` — products of 1-4 variables (with replacement)
288: - **Coefficient-scaled products**: `with_c_xs1_muls` through `with_c_xs4_muls` — `C * variable_product`
289: - **Function expressions**: `wout_c_linear_funcs`, `wout_c_nonlin_funcs`, `with_c_linear_funcs`, `with_c_nonlin_funcs`
290:   - Linear: `f(var_product)`, `f(var_product)` with inverse
291:   - Nonlinear: `f(C*var_product + C)`, with inverse
292: - **Expansion term pools**: `var_sub_terms`, `add_extend_terms`, `mul_extend_terms` — vary by complexity level (low/med/high)
293: 
294: **Key methods:**
295: 
296: - **`first_exprs()`**: Generate initial generation. Combines variable products + function expressions, adds `+C` variants, uniquifies via `evalf()` hashing, wraps in `Model` objects with `gen_relation="first_gen"`
297: - **`grow(M)`**: Expand a single model via 5 operators:
298:   1. **`_var_sub()`**: Variable substitution — replaces input variable occurrences with more complex expressions (recursive, depth-limited)
299:   2. **`_add_extend()`**: Addition extension — adds terms to `Add` nodes (recursive)
300:   3. **`_mul_extend()`**: Multiplication extension — adds factors to `Mul` nodes (recursive)
301:   4. **`_add_extend_top_level()`**: Top-level addition extension with more complex multiplication (non-recursive)
302:   5. **`_shrinker()`**: Term removal from `Add` nodes (recursive)
303: - **`_toggle_plus_C(expr)`**: Adds or removes a bare `C` from an addition
304: - **`_uniquify(exprs)`**: Removes duplicates via `p.evalf()` hashing
305: 
306: **Policy levels** (all configurable via kwargs):
307: - `func_level`: "linear" or "nonlin" — whether functions use affine transforms `f(C*x+C)` or just `f(x)`
308: - `init_level`: "low", "med", "high" — complexity of first-generation models
309: - `grow_level` / `subs_level` / `adds_level` / `muls_level`: expansion complexity levels
310: - `add_xtop`: Whether to extend at the top level of additions
311: - `shrinker`: Whether to try removing terms from additions
312: - `limiting_depth`: Depth limit for variable substitution (default 4)
313: - `grow_filter`: Whether to avoid duplicate terms in additions
314: 
315: #### 3. Multi-Objective Selection (`pypge/selection.py`)
316: 
317: Taken from DEAP. Key functions:
318: 
319: - **`selNSGA2(individuals, k, nd='standard')`**: NSGA-II selection. Sorts into Pareto fronts, assigns crowding distances, fills selection from best fronts, breaking ties by crowding distance.
320:   - `nd='standard'`: Uses `sortNondominated()` (O(M*N^2))
321:   - `nd='log'`: Uses `sortLogNondominated()` — **this is what PGE uses**
322: - **`sortLogNondominated(individuals, k)`**: Generalized Reduced Run-Time Complexity Non-Dominated Sorting (Fortin et al. 2013). Uses recursive divide-and-conquer with sweep procedures (`sweepA`, `sweepB`) for O(N log^(M-1) N) complexity.
323: - **`assignCrowdingDist(individuals)`**: Assigns crowding distance to each individual for diversity maintenance.
324: - **`selSPEA2(individuals, k)`**: Strength Pareto EA II selection.
325: - **`isDominated(wvalues1, wvalues2)`**: Checks if wvalues1 is dominated by wvalues2 (minimization semantics: lower is better).
326: 
327: Fitness objects need `values` attribute (tuple) for `selNSGA2` and `wvalues` attribute for `sortLogNondominated`.
328: 
329: #### 4. Fitness Calculation (`pypge/fitness_funcs.py`)
330: 
331: Dynamically constructs multi-objective fitness from parameter list like `["normalize", "-(1)jpsz", "-score", "+bic"]`:
332: 
333: - Weight parsing: `"-(1)jpsz"` → weight = -1.0 (minimize jpsz), `"+bic"` → weight = +1.0 (maximize bic)
334: - `"normalize"` prefix: normalizes each objective across the population by L2 norm before setting fitness values
335: - `build_value_extractor(params)`: creates a function that extracts specified attributes from each model
336: - Fitness values are set via `modl.fitness.setValues(vals)` on DEAP-style fitness objects
337: 
338: For JAX port, fitness values can be stored directly as tuples on model objects — no DEAP dependency needed.
339: 
340: #### 5. Expression Filters (`pypge/filters.py`)
341: 
342: `default_filters` list applied to every model:
343: 
344: - `filter_too_big`: Removes models with `size() > 64`
345: - `filter_has_int_coeff`: Removes expressions with hardcoded integer coefficients (not using `C` symbols)
346: - `filter_has_big_pow`: Removes expressions with power exponents > 6
347: - `filter_just_C`: Removes expressions that are just the coefficient symbol `C` or a number
348: - `filter_no_C`: Removes expressions with no coefficients (constant expressions)
349: - `filter_has_coeff_pow`: Removes expressions like `C^2` (coefficient raised to a power)
350: 
351: Filter API: each filter takes `(modl, expr)` and returns `True` if the expression should be **rejected**. Walks `sympy.preorder_traversal(expr)` and checks each node.
352: 
353: #### 6. Algebraic Manipulation (`pypge/algebra.py`)
354: 
355: Applies symbolic simplification to expressions:
356: 
357: - **`manip_model(modl, method)`**: Applies method to model. Returns `(new_model, None)` if expression changed, `(None, "same")` if unchanged, `(None, error)` on failure.
358: - **`do_simp(expr, method)`**: Supports `"simplify"`, `"expand"`, `"factor"`
359: - Methods: `sympy.simplify()`, `sympy.expand()`, `sympy.factor()`
360: 
361: #### 7. Memoization / Deduplication (`pypge/memoize.py`)
362: 
363: - **`Memoizer`**: Indexes models by expression hash. `insert(model)` returns `True` if new, `False` if duplicate. `lookup(model)` returns `(found, model)`.
364: - **`Mapper`**: Maps sympy node types to integer codes for serialization (for remote evaluation). Not needed in JAX port — use `hash(expr)` or `expr.__hash__()` directly.
365: - In the JAX port, deduplication can use a simple `dict[expr_hash: Expr] -> Model` mapping.
366: 
367: #### 8. The PGE Search Class (`pypge/search.py`)
368: 
369: The `PGE` class orchestrates everything. Key data structures:
370: 
371: - **`self.models`**: All models ever created (indexed by `id`)
372: - **`self.hmap`**: Dict mapping `expr -> Model` for deduplication
373: - **`self.final`**: All fully evaluated, finalized models
374: - **`self.nsga2_list`**: Models waiting to be expanded (the "population" heap)
375: - **`self.nsga2_peek`**: Models that have been peek-evaluated, waiting for full evaluation
376: - **`self.multi_expanders[i]`**: Per-expander config with `pop_count`, `nsga2_list`, and `grower`
377: 
378: **Main loop per iteration:**
379: 
380: 1. **Multi-expand**: For each expander, pop `pop_count` models via NSGA-II selection, call `grower.grow()`, push remaining back
381: 2. **Filter**: Remove invalid models
382: 3. **Memoize**: Deduplicate via expression hash
383: 4. **Algebra**: Apply expand/factor to unique models
384: 5. **Filter + Memoize** algebraic results again
385: 6. **Peek-evaluate** unique models on subset of data
386: 7. **Push** peek'd models to `nsga2_peek` heap
387: 8. **Pop** best models from peek heap for full evaluation (via NSGA-II selection)
388: 9. **Full-evaluate** selected models on full training data
389: 10. **Push** to `self.final` and `nsga2_list`
390: 
391: **Progressive evaluation**: Uses `peek_npts` (default 16) data points for fast partial evaluation, then selects best models from peek heap for full evaluation on all data.
392: 
393: ### Data Flow for Each Model
394: 
395: ```
396: 1. Creation: Grower.first_exprs() or Grower.grow() → sympy.Expr
397: 2. Model wrapping: Model(expr) → rewrite_coeff(), compute Jacobian
398: 3. Filtering: filters.filter_models() → remove invalid expressions
399: 4. Deduplication: memoize_models() → check self.hmap[expr]
400: 5. Algebra: algebra.manip_model() → expand/factor
401: 6. Deduplication again: after algebra
402: 7. Peek evaluation: eval_model() on subset of data (fast)
403: 8. Selection: selNSGA2() or sortLogNondominated() picks best peek'd models
404: 9. Full evaluation: eval_model() on full data (slow, with lmfit)
405: 10. Fitness assignment: fitness_funcs.build_fitness_calc() sets model.fitness.values
406: 11. Population update: push to nsga2_list for future expansion or final for output
407: ```
408: 
409: ### JAX Port Design Decisions
410: 
411: Key differences from pypge for the JAX port:
412: 
413: 1. **No DEAP dependency** — fitness values stored directly as tuples on model objects
414: 2. **No multiprocessing by default** — JAX handles parallelism via XLA; can add later
415: 3. **No remote evaluation** — all computation is local via JAX
416: 4. **No lmfit** — replaced by custom JAX-native LM optimizer
417: 5. **No sklearn** — replaced by JAX-native metrics
418: 6. **No `lmfit.Parameters`** — coefficients stored as `jnp.ndarray`
419: 7. **Model class** — can be simplified; state flags are important for the search loop but the DEAP-style fitness wrapper is not needed
420: 
421: ### Dependencies
422: 
423: Current `pyproject.toml` dependencies:
424: - `jax`, `jaxlib` — array computation + autodiff
425: - `numpy` — numeric operations
426: - `scipy` — for `jax.scipy.optimize.minimize`
427: - `sympy` — symbolic expression representation
428: - `networkx` — graph storage (for relationship tracking)
429: - `tqdm` — progress bars
430: 
431: Optional deps (not needed for core PGE loop):
432: - `scikit-learn`, `lmfit`, `pandas` — benchmark/compatibility only
433: 
434: ### Porting Order (Recommended)
435: 
436: 1. **`filters.py`** — Simple, no dependencies on other new modules
437: 2. **`algebra.py`** — Simple, only depends on sympy
438: 3. **`memoize.py`** — Simple hash-based dedup
439: 4. **`fitness_funcs.py`** — Multi-objective fitness construction (no DEAP needed)
440: 5. **`selection.py`** — NSGA-II / SPEA-II (standalone, no other new deps)
441: 6. **`expand.py`** — Grower class (depends on filters for `_uniquify`, creates Model objects)
442: 7. **`model.py`** — Simplified Model class for the search loop (state tracking, size metrics)
443: 8. **`search.py`** — PGE class (depends on all above)
444: 9. **`parallel.py`** — Multiprocessing (optional, can skip initially)

(End of file - total 444 lines)
</content>
```

57: ## Architecture
58: 
59: ```
60: sympy.Expr → SearchModel → Grower.first_exprs() → Filter → Memoize → Algebra
61:                                                         → Filter → Memoize
62:                                                         → PGE._eval_models() (peek)
63:                                                         → PGE._peek_pop() (NSGA-II)
64:                                                         → PGE._eval_models() (full)
65:                                                         → PGE._final_push() → final list
66: ```
67: 
68: ### Key Design Decisions
69: 
70: 1. **No DEAP dependency** — fitness values stored as tuples on model objects (`fitness_values`, `wvalues`)
71: 2. **No multiprocessing** — JAX/XLA handles parallelism; skipped for now
72: 3. **No remote evaluation** — all computation is local via JAX
73: 4. **No lmfit/sklearn** — replaced by JAX-native LM optimizer + JAX metrics
74: 5. **Two model classes**: `JAXModel` (pure JAX evaluation) + `SearchModel` (search loop state)

93: ## Quick Start
94: 
95: ```python
96: import numpy as np
97: from pge_jax import PGE
98: 
99: # Generate synthetic data
100: np.random.seed(42)
101: X = np.random.randn(100, 2)
102: Y = 3.0 * X[:, 0] + 1.5 * X[:, 1]**2 - 0.5 * np.sin(X[:, 0])
103: 
104: # Run PGE search
105: pge = PGE(
106:     usable_vars=["x0", "x1"],
107:     usable_funcs=["sin", "cos", "exp", "log"],
108:     max_iter=10,
109:     pop_count=3,
110:     peek_npts=16,
111: )
112: pge.fit(X, Y)
113: 
114: # Get results
115: paretos = pge.get_final_paretos()
116: best = pge.get_best_model()
117: print(best.pretty_expr())

<content>
1: """Search-loop-aware model with state tracking and size metrics.
2: 
3: This is the PGE search-loop equivalent of pypge's ``Model`` class.
4: It wraps a sympy expression, manages lifecycle state flags, computes
5: tree-size metrics, and holds fitness values for multi-objective
6: selection.
7: 
8: Unlike :class:`JAXModel` (which is the pure JAX evaluation wrapper),
9: this class is designed to be passed through the full PGE pipeline:
10: filtering, memoization, expansion, evaluation, and selection.
11: """
12: 
13: from __future__ import annotations
14: 
15: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Optional, Tuple
16: 
17: import sympy
18: 
19: if TYPE_CHECKING:
20:     from pge_jax.model import JAXModel
21: 
22: 
23: class SearchModel:
24:     """Wraps a sympy expression and manages its search-loop lifecycle.
25: 
26:     Parameters
27:     ----------
28:     expr:
29:         A sympy expression.  Bare ``sympy.Symbol('C')`` leaves are
30:         treated as optimisable coefficients; all other free symbols
31:         are input variables.
32:     xs:
33:         Explicit list of input-variable symbols.  If ``None`` they
34:         are inferred from *expr*.
35:     cs:
36:         Explicit list of coefficient symbols.  If ``None`` they are
37:         inferred from *expr*.
38:     p_id:
39:         Parent model ID (-2 for root/first-generation models).
40:     reln:
41:         Generation relation string (e.g. ``"first_gen"``,
42:         ``"var_xpnd"``, ``"add_xpnd"``, ``"mul_xpnd"``, ``"shrunk"``).
43: 
44:     Attributes
45:     ----------

47:         Unique model ID (assigned by :class:`Memoizer`).
48:     iter_id : int
49:         Iteration in which this model was created.
50:     parent_id : int
51:         Parent model ID.
52:     gen_relation : str
53:         How this model was generated.
54:     orig : sympy.Expr
55:         Original expression before coefficient rewriting.
56:     expr : sympy.Expr
57:         Expanded expression after ``rewrite_coeff()``.
58:     xs : list[sympy.Symbol]
59:         Input variable symbols.
60:     cs : list[sympy.Symbol]
61:         Coefficient symbols (``C_0, C_1, ...``).
62:     jax_model : JAXModel | None
63:         The underlying JAX evaluation wrapper (built lazily).
64:     sz : int

77:         Full fitness computed on all training data.
78:     improve_score, improve_r2, improve_evar, improve_aic, improve_bic, improve_redchi : float
79:         Improvement over parent model.
80:     fitness_values : tuple[float, ...]
81:         Raw fitness values for selection.
82:     wvalues : tuple[float, ...]
83:         Weighted fitness values (sign × value).
84:     crowding_dist : float
85:         Crowding distance for diversity maintenance.
86:     """
87: 
88:     # Lifecycle state flags
89:     inited: bool
90:     memoized: bool

121:         self.peek_queued = False
122:         self.peek_popped = False
123:         self.evaluated = False
124:         self.queued = False
125:         self.popped = False
126:         self.expanded = False
127:         self.finalized = False
128:         self.errored = False
129:

131:         self.orig: sympy.Expr = expr
132:         self.expr: sympy.Expr = sympy.expand(expr)

134: 
135:         # Variables and coefficients
136:         self.xs: list = list(xs) if xs is not None else []
137:         self.cs: list = list(cs) if cs is not None else []
138: 
139:         # JAX evaluation wrapper (built lazily)
140:         self.jax_model: Optional[JAXModel] = None
141: 
142:         # Size metrics
143:         self.sz: int = 0
144:         self.psz: int = 0
145:         self.jsz: int = 0
146:         self.jpsz: int = 0
147:         self.ncs: int = len(self.cs)
148: 
149:         # Peek (partial) fitness

151:         self.peek_r2: Optional[float] = None
152:         self.peek_evar: Optional[float] = None
153:         self.peek_aic: Optional[float] = None
154:         self.peek_bic: Optional[float] = None
155:         self.peek_redchi: Optional[float] = None
156: 
157:         # Full fitness

160:         self.evar: Optional[float] = None
161:         self.aic: Optional[float] = None
162:         self.bic: Optional[float] = None

164:         self.redchi: Optional[float] = None
165:         self.mae: Optional[float] = None
166:         self.rmae: Optional[float] = None
167: 
168:         # Improvement over parent
169:         self.improve_score: Optional[float] = None
170:         self.improve_r2: Optional[float] = None
171:         self.improve_evar: Optional[float] = None
172:         self.improve_aic: Optional[float] = None
173:         self.improve_bic: Optional[float] = None
174:         self.improve_redchi: Optional[float] = None
175: 
176:         # Fitness for selection
177:         self.fitness_values: Tuple[float, ...] = ()
178:         self.wvalues: Tuple[float, ...] = ()
179:         self.crowding_dist: float = 0.0
180: 
181:         # Fit bookkeeping
182:         self.peek_nfev: int = 0
183:         self.eval_nfev: int = 0
184:         self.total_fev: int = 0
185: 
186:         # All done
187:         self.inited = True
188: 
189:     def __hash__(self) -> int:
190:         return self.id
191: 
192:     @property
193:     def values(self) -> Tuple[float, ...]:
194:         """Raw fitness values for DEAP-style selection compatibility."""
195:         return self.fitness_values
196: 
197:     def __str__(self) -> str:
198:         if self.pretty is None:
199:             self.pretty_expr()
200:         fs = (
201:             "{:5d}  {:5d}  {:5d}    {:2d}   {:2d}   {:2d}   {:2d}"
202:             "  {:15.6f}  {:10.6f}  {:10.6f}  {:15.6f}  {:15.6f}  {:15.6f}  |  {:s}"
203:         )
204:         return fs.format(
205:             self.id,
206:             self.iter_id,
207:             self.parent_id,
208:             self.size(),
209:             self.psz,
210:             self.jsz,
211:             self.jpsz,
212:             self.score or 0,
213:             self.r2 or 0,
214:             self.evar or 0,
215:             self.aic or 0,
216:             self.bic or 0,
217:             self.redchi or 0,
218:             self.pretty,
219:         )
220: 
221:     def pretty_expr(self, float_format: str = "%.4e") -> str:
222:         """Substitute fitted coefficient values into the expression."""
223:         if self.jax_model is not None and self.jax_model.c_values is not None:
224:             subs = dict(zip(self.cs, self.jax_model.c_values.tolist()[: self.ncs]))
225:             self.pretty = str(self.expr.subs(subs))
226:         else:
227:             self.pretty = str(self.expr)
228:         return self.pretty
229: 
230:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
231:     # Size calculation
232:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
233: 
234:     def size(self) -> int:
235:         """Return the tree size, computing it lazily if needed."""
236:         if self.sz == 0:
237:             self.sz, self.psz = self.calc_tree_size()
238:             self.jsz, self.jpsz = self.calc_jac_size()
239:         return self.sz
240: 
241:     def calc_tree_size(self) -> Tuple[int, int]:
242:         """Compute tree size and penalised tree size.
243: 
244:         Walks ``sympy.preorder_traversal``, counts nodes, and adds
245:         +2 penalty per function node.  Integer leaf values are added
246:         as their absolute value.
247: 
248:         Returns
249:         -------
250:         tuple[int, int]
251:             ``(size, penalised_size)``.
252:         """
253:         i = 0
254:         p = 0
255:         for e in sympy.preorder_traversal(self.expr):
256:             if e.is_Integer:
257:                 i += int(abs(e))
258:                 continue
259:             if e.is_Function:
260:                 p += 2
261:             i += 1
262:         return i, i + p
263: 
264:     def calc_jac_size(self) -> Tuple[int, int]:
265:         """Compute Jacobian size and penalised Jacobian size.
266: 
267:         Returns
268:         -------
269:         tuple[int, int]
270:             ``(size, penalised_size)``.
271:         """
272:         # Build the Jacobian symbolically
273:         if len(self.cs) == 0:
274:             return 0, 0
275:         jac_exprs = [sympy.diff(self.expr, c) for c in self.cs]
276:         i, p = 0, 0
277:         for jac in jac_exprs:
278:             for e in sympy.preorder_traversal(jac):
279:                 if e.is_Integer:
280:                     i += int(abs(e))
281:                     continue
282:                 if e.is_Function:
283:                     p += 2
284:                 i += 1
285:         return i, i + p
286: 
287:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
288:     # Coefficient rewriting (converts bare C to C_0, C_1, ...)
289:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
290: 
291:     def rewrite_coeff(self) -> None:
292:         """Rewrite bare ``sympy.Symbol('C')`` into ``C_0, C_1, ...``.
293: 
294:         Replaces all bare ``C`` atoms in ``self.orig`` with
295:         sequentially-numbered coefficient symbols, updates
296:         ``self.expr`` and ``self.cs``, and builds the JAX wrapper.
297:         """
298:         from pge_jax.model import JAXModel as _JAXModel
299: 
300:         ii = 0
301:         expr, ii = self._rewrite_coeff_helper(self.orig, 0)
302:         self.expr = expr
303:         self.cs = [sympy.Symbol(f"C_{i}") for i in range(ii)]
304:         self.ncs = len(self.cs)
305: 
306:         # Build JAX wrapper
307:         self.jax_model = _JAXModel(expr, cs=self.cs, xs=self.xs)
308: 
309:     def _rewrite_coeff_helper(self, expr, ii: int):
310:         """Recursive helper for :meth:`rewrite_coeff`."""
311:         ret = expr
312:         if not expr.is_Atom:
313:             args = []
314:             for e in expr.args:
315:                 if not e.is_Atom:
316:                     ee, ii = self._rewrite_coeff_helper(e, ii)
317:                     args.append(ee)
318:                 elif e == sympy.Symbol("C"):
319:                     args.append(sympy.Symbol(f"C_{ii}"))
320:                     ii += 1
321:                 else:
322:                     args.append(e)
323:             args = tuple(args)
324:             ret = expr.func(*args)
325:         return ret, ii
326: 
327:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
328:     # Fitness comparison helpers
329:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
330: 
331:     def dominates(self, other: "SearchModel") -> bool:
332:         """Check if this model dominates *other* in fitness.
333: 
334:         Uses weighted fitness values (``wvalues``).  A model dominates
335:         another if it is no worse in all objectives and strictly better
336:         in at least one (minimisation semantics: lower is better).
337: 
338:         Parameters
339:         ----------
340:         other:
341:             Another model to compare against.
342: 
343:         Returns
344:         -------
345:         bool
346:             ``True`` if this model dominates *other*.
347:         """
348:         if not hasattr(other, "wvalues") or not self.wvalues:
349:             return False
350:         not_equal = False
351:         for self_w, other_w in zip(self.wvalues, other.wvalues):
352:             if self_w > other_w:
353:                 return False
354:             if self_w < other_w:
355:                 not_equal = True
356:         return not_equal

(End of file - total 356 lines)
</content>

{
  "content": "# pge-jax\n\nJAX implementation of the **Prioritized Grammar Enumeration (PGE)** algorithm for symbolic regression.\n\n## Overview\n\npge-jax is a complete symbolic regression system that automatically discovers mathematical formulas from data. It enumerates candidate expressions from a grammar, fits their coefficients using JAX-native Levenberg-Marquardt optimization, and selects the best models using multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (NSGA-II).\n\nThe key advantage over prior implementations (pypge, go-pge) is a fully JAX-native evaluation pipeline, enabling:\n\n- **GPU/TPU acceleration** of model evaluation and Jacobian computation\n- **JIT compilation** via `jax.jit` and `jax.vmap`\n- **Automatic differentiation** for efficient gradient-based optimization\n- **No external ML dependencies** — no scikit-learn, lmfit, or DEAP required\n\n## Quick Start\n\n```python\nimport jax\njax.config.update(\"jax_enable_x64\", True)\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom pge_jax import PGE\n\n# Generate synthetic data\nnp.random.seed(42)\nX = np.random.randn(100, 2)\nY = 3.0 * X[:, 0] + 1.5 * X[:, 1]**2 - 0.5 * np.sin(X[:, 0])\n\n# Run PGE search\npge = PGE(\n    usable_vars=[\"x0\", \"x1\"],\n    usable_funcs=[\"sin\", \"cos\", \"exp\", \"log\"],\n    max_iter=10,\n    pop_count=3,\n    peek_npts=16,       # subset size for fast partial evaluation\n)\npge.fit(X, Y)\n\n# Get results\nbest = pge.get_best_model()\nprint(best.pretty_expr())  # e.g. \"3.0*x0 + 1.5*x1**2 - 0.5*sin(x0)\"\n\nparetos = pge.get_final_paretos()  # list of Pareto fronts\n```\n\n## Architecture\n\n```\npge_jax/\n├── __init__.py          # Public API exports\n├── model.py             # JAXModel — sympy expression → JAX evaluation wrapper\n├── optimize.py          # Levenberg-Marquardt + BFGS optimizers (JAX-native)\n├── metrics.py           # JAX-native regression metrics (RMSE, R², AIC, etc.)\n├── evaluate.py          # High-level fit/predict/evaluate pipeline\n├── search_model.py      # SearchModel — expression state, size metrics, fitness\n├── filters.py           # Expression validity filters (size, coefficients, powers)\n├── algebra.py           # Symbolic expand/factor/simplify\n├── memoize.py           # Hash-based expression deduplication\n├── fitness_funcs.py     # Multi-objective fitness construction\n├── selection.py         # NSGA-II, SPEA-II, log-ND sort (from DEAP)\n├── expand.py            # Grower — grammar-based expression enumeration\n└── search.py            # PGE — main search loop orchestration\n```\n\n## Public API\n\n### `PGE` — End-to-End Search\n\nThe primary entry point. Wraps the full search pipeline:\n\n```python\nfrom pge_jax import PGE\n\npge = PGE(\n    usable_vars=[\"x0\", \"x1\"],   # or \"x0 x1\" or list of sympy.Symbol\n    usable_funcs=[\"sin\", \"cos\", \"exp\", \"log\", \"tan\", \"sqrt\"],\n    max_iter=100,               # data points for fast partial (peek) evaluation\n    max_size=64,                # max expression tree size\n    max_power=5,                # max power exponent\n    algebra_methods=[\"expand\", \"factor\"],\n    err_method=\"mse\",           # error metric for score\n    random_seed=23,\n)\n\npge.fit(X_train, Y_train)          # sklearn-style: returns self\nbest = pge.get_best_model()        # SearchModel with lowest score\nparetos = pge.get_final_paretos()  # list[list[SearchModel]]\n```\n\n### `SearchModel` — Expression State\n\nWraps a sympy expression with lifecycle state, size metrics, and fitness:\n\n```python\nfrom pge_jax import SearchModel\nimport sympy\n\nx = sympy.Symbol(\"x\")\nc0 = sympy.Symbol(\"C_0\")\nexpr = c0 * x + 1\n\nmodel = SearchModel(expr, xs=[x], cs=[c0])\nmodel.rewrite_coeff()   # builds JAXModel wrapper, converts bare C → C_0, C_1, ...\n\nmodel.size()            # tree size\nmodel.psz               # penalised size (+2 per function node)\nmodel.jpsz              # penalised Jacobian size\nmodel.score             # RMSE after fitting\nmodel.r2                # R-squared\nmodel.pretty_expr()     # expression with fitted coefficients substituted\n```\n\n### `JAXModel` — Pure JAX Evaluation\n\nFor users who want to evaluate a specific expression without the search loop:\n\n```python\nfrom pge_jax import JAXModel, fit_model, evaluate\nimport jax.numpy as jnp\nimport sympy\n\nx = sympy.Symbol(\"x\")\nc0, c1 = sympy.symbols(\"C_0 C_1\")\nexpr = c0 * x + c1\n\nmodel = JAXModel(expr)\nresult = fit_model(model, jnp.array([3.0, 5.0, 7.0]), jnp.array(x_data))\nprint(result.coefficients)  # [2.0, 1.0]\n\neval_result = evaluate(model, jnp.array(y_true), result.predictions)\nprint(f\"R²: {eval_result.r2:.4f}\")\n```\n\n### Individual Components\n\nAll modules are importable independently:\n\n```python\nfrom pge_jax import (\n    # Filters\n    filter_models, default_filters,\n\n    # Algebra\n    manip_model, do_simp,\n\n    # Memoization\n    Memoizer,\n\n    # Selection\n    selNSGA2, selSPEA2, sortLogNondominated, isDominated, assignCrowdingDist,\n\n    # Fitness\n    build_fitness_calc, build_fitness_weights, build_value_extractor,\n\n    # Expansion\n    Grower, map_names_to_funcs,\n\n    # Metrics\n    rmse, mae, mse, r2, explained_variance, aic, bic, chisqr, redchi, rmae,\n\n    # Optimizers\n    fit_levenberg_marquardt, fit_least_squares,\n)\n```\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n### Why sympy + JAX?\n\nSympy handles expression representation, tree manipulation, expansion, and simplification. JAX replaces the evaluation and optimization pipeline, providing GPU acceleration and automatic differentiation.\n\n### No DEAP Dependency\n\nFitness values are stored directly as tuples on `SearchModel` objects (`fitness_values`, `wvalues`, `crowding_dist`). Selection functions expect these attributes instead of DEAP's `Fitness` wrapper.\n\n### Two Model Classes\n\n- **`JAXModel`** — Pure JAX evaluation wrapper (sympy → JAX, predict, jacobian)\n- **`SearchModel`** — Search-loop state machine (lifecycle flags, size metrics, fitness, selection compatibility)\n\n### Levenberg-Marquardt\n\nThe default optimizer because it's well-suited for least-squares problems, uses the JAX-computed Jacobian efficiently, and matches the original pypge approach.\n\n### Progressive Evaluation\n\nThe search uses `peek_npts` (default 16) data points for fast partial evaluation of candidate expressions, then fully evaluates only the most promising ones on all training data. This dramatically reduces the number of expensive full evaluations.\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\n# Create virtual environment\npython3 -m venv .venv\nsource .venv/bin/activate\n\n# Install from source\npip install -e \".[dev]\"\n\n# Or with benchmark dependencies (for pypge compatibility)\npip install -e \".[dev,benchmark]\"\n```\n\n### Optional Dependencies\n\n| Group | Packages | Purpose |\n|-------|----------|---------|\n| `dev` | pytest, ruff, mypy, pre-commit | Development tooling |\n| `benchmark` | scikit-learn, lmfit, pandas | Compatibility with pypge benchmarks |\n| `notebook` | jupyter, matplotlib | Interactive exploration |\n\n## Development\n\n```bash\n# Run all tests\npython -m pytest tests/ -v\n\n# Lint\nruff check pge_jax/ tests/\n\n# Format\nruff format pge_jax/ tests/\n\n# Type check\nmypy pge_jax/\n```\n\n### Configuration\n\n- **Line length:** 120 characters\n- **Target Python:** 3.11+\n- **Linter:** ruff (E, F, I, N, W, NPY rules)\n- **Type checker:** mypy (non-strict mode)\n- **JAX float64:** Enable with `jax.config.update(\"jax_enable_x64\", True)` or `JAX_ENABLE_X64=1` env var\n\n## Prior Art\n\n- **pypge**: Original Python implementation — <https://github.com/verdverm/pypge>\n- **go-pge**: Go implementation with performance optimizations — <https://github.com/verdverm/go-pge>\n- **PySR**: Symbolic regression with JAX — <https://github.com/MilesCranmer/pysr>\n- **FFX**: Fast feature selection for symbolic regression — <https://github.com/ffx-org/ffx>\n\n## Citation\n\n> \"Prioritized Grammar Enumeration\" — Best Paper, GECCO 2013\n> <http://dl.acm.org/citation.cfm?id=2463486>\n",

  "content": "# pge-jax — Agent Instructions\n\n## Project Structure\n\n```\npge-jax/\n├── pge_jax/          # Package source\n│   ├── __init__.py   # Public API — add new exports here\n│   ├── model.py      # JAXModel: sympy → JAX evaluation wrapper\n│   ├── optimize.py   # LM and BFGS optimizers\n│   ├── metrics.py    # JAX-native regression metrics\n│   ├── evaluate.py   # High-level fit/predict/evaluate pipeline\n│   ├── search_model.py  # SearchModel: state, size metrics, fitness\n│   ├── filters.py    # Expression validity filters\n│   ├── algebra.py    # Symbolic expand/factor/simplify\n│   ├── memoize.py    # Hash-based expression deduplication\n│   ├── fitness_funcs.py  # Multi-objective fitness construction\n│   ├── selection.py  # NSGA-II, SPEA-II, log-ND sort\n│   ├── expand.py     # Grower: grammar-based expression enumeration\n│   └── search.py     # PGE: main search loop orchestration\n├── tests/            # pytest test suite\n├── pyproject.toml    # Build config, deps, tool settings\n├── README.md         # User-facing documentation\n└── AGENTS.md         # This file\n```\n\n## Running the Code\n\n```bash\n# Enter the venv (created during setup)\nsource .venv/bin/activate\n\n# Run all tests\npython -m pytest tests/ -v\n\n# Run a single test file\npython -m pytest tests/test_search.py -v\n\n# Run a single test\npython -m pytest tests/test_search.py::TestIntegration::test_pge_single_var -v\n\n# Lint\nruff check pge_jax/ tests/\n\n# Format\nruff format pge_jax/ tests/\n\n# Type check\nmypy pge_jax/\n```\n\n## Coding Conventions\n\n- **Python 3.11+** — use modern syntax: `X | Y` unions, `match`/`case`, `typing.Self`\n- **120-char line limit** — configured in `pyproject.toml`\n- **Docstrings** — Google style (parameters, returns, raises sections)\n- **Imports** — standard library first, then third-party, then local (`pge_jax.*`), alphabetized within groups\n- **No bare `import jax`** — always `import jax.numpy as jnp` for array ops\n- **Type hints** — preferred on all public functions and class attributes\n- **No print statements** in library code — use logging or return values\n\n## Core Architecture\n\n### Two Abstraction Layers\n\n**Layer 1: Evaluation** (`JAXModel` + `optimize.py` + `metrics.py`)\n- Wraps a sympy expression, provides JAX-compatible predict/jacobian\n- Fits coefficients via Levenberg-Marquardt (JAX-native)\n- Computes regression metrics (RMSE, R², AIC, BIC, etc.)\n\n**Layer 2: Search** (`SearchModel` + `PGE` + selection + expansion)\n- `SearchModel`: wraps expression with lifecycle state flags, size metrics, fitness values\n- `PGE`: orchestrates the full search loop (generate → filter → memoize → algebra → evaluate → select → expand)\n- `Grower`: grammar-based expression enumeration with 5 operators (var_sub, add_extend, mul_extend, add_xtop, shrink)\n\n### Evaluation Pipeline\n\n```\nsympy.Expr → JAXModel.__init__() → jax_fun, jac_fun\n                                 → fit_levenberg_marquardt()\n                                 → FitResult(coefficients, predictions, cost, ...)\n                                 → evaluate() → EvalResult(all metrics)\n```\n\n### Search Pipeline\n\n```\nsympy.Expr → SearchModel → Grower.first_exprs() → Filter → Memoize → Algebra\n                                                         → Filter → Memoize\n                                                         → PGE._eval_models() (peek)\n                                                         → PGE._peek_pop() (NSGA-II)\n                                                         → PGE._eval_models() (full)\n                                                         → PGE._final_push() → final list\n```\n\n### Key Types\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass FitResult:\n    success: bool\n    coefficients: jnp.ndarray   # optimized coefficients\n    predictions: jnp.ndarray    # model predictions at optimized coeffs\n    cost: float                 # sum of squared residuals\n    n_residuals: int\n    n_params: int\n    message: str = \"\"\n    nfev: int = 0\n\n@dataclass\nclass EvalResult:\n    fit: FitResult\n    score: float        # RMSE\n    r2: float\n    evar: float\n    aic: float\n    bic: float\n    chisqr: float\n    redchi: float\n    mae: float\n    rmae: float\n    predictions: jnp.ndarray\n```\n\n## Gotchas\n\n### JAX float64\n\nJAX defaults to float32 on most platforms. To use float64 you need:\n\n```python\njax.config.update(\"jax_enable_x64\", True)\n```\n\nOr set the env var: `JAX_ENABLE_X64=1`. The code requests float64 in `jnp.asarray(..., dtype=jnp.float64)` which triggers warnings when x64 is disabled. Tests pass with float32, but precision-sensitive work (e.g., symbolic regression convergence) may need x64.\n\n### sympy.lambdify + JAX\n\n- `sympy.lambdify` with `modules=\"jax\"` works for most expressions but falls back to numpy on failure.\n- Each coefficient symbol becomes a separate argument. The wrapper in `JAXModel.jax_fun` unpacks the coefficient array to match.\n- If the expression has no variables (constant), `jax_fun` receives no input arrays — handle this case.\n\n### LM Optimizer Convergence\n\nThe LM implementation has multiple convergence criteria:\n1. Cost below tolerance (`cost < tol`)\n2. Relative cost change below tolerance\n3. Coefficient change below tolerance\n4. Damping blowup (`mu > 1e12`) — failure\n\nThe default `tol=1e-4` works for most cases. The float32 precision means you won't get better than ~1e-6 accuracy regardless.\n\n### Coefficient Symbol Convention\n\nCoefficients are identified by name prefix: `C_` or `C[`. The `SearchModel.rewrite_coeff()` method converts bare `sympy.Symbol('C')` leaves into `C_0`, `C_1`, etc. If you create expressions with bare `C` symbols, they won't be extracted as coefficients unless `rewrite_coeff()` is called.\n\n### Test Precision\n\nTests use `atol=5e-3` or `rel=5e-3` tolerances because float32 limits precision. Don't tighten these without first ensuring x64 is enabled.\n\n### Selection API Compatibility\n\nThe `selection.py` functions expect specific attributes on model objects:\n- `selNSGA2` / `assignCrowdingDist` — expects `individual.values` (tuple of raw fitness)\n- `sortLogNondominated` — expects `individual.wvalues` (tuple of weighted fitness)\n- `SearchModel` provides both: `values` property returns `fitness_values`, `wvalues` is a direct attribute\n\n### Empty Population Edge Cases\n\n`selNSGA2` and `sortLogNondominated` return early (empty list) when given an empty individuals list. The PGE search loop may pass empty lists when the population is exhausted — callers should handle this.\n\n## Adding New Code\n\n### New Metric\n\n1. Add function to `pge_jax/metrics.py` with Google-style docstring\n2. Add import and export in `pge_jax/__init__.py`\n3. Add to `EvalResult` in `pge_jax/evaluate.py` if it should be part of the full evaluation\n4. Add tests in `tests/test_metrics.py`\n\n### New Optimizer\n\n1. Add function to `pge_jax/optimize.py` — return `FitResult`\n2. Add import in `pge_jax/__init__.py`\n3. Wire into `fit_model()` in `pge_jax/evaluate.py` if it should be a first-class option\n4. Add tests in `tests/test_optimize.py`\n\n### New Model Feature\n\n1. Modify `JAXModel` in `pge_jax/model.py`\n2. Update `_build_jax_functions()` if the change affects evaluation\n3. Add tests in `tests/test_model.py`\n\n### New Search Module\n\n1. Add to `pge_jax/` with Google-style docstring\n2. Add exports in `pge_jax/__init__.py`\n3. Add tests in `tests/test_search.py`\n4. Wire into `PGE` class in `pge_jax/search.py` if it should be a first-class option\n\n### New Filter\n\n1. Add function to `pge_jax/filters.py` — takes `(modl: SearchModel, expr)` returns `True` if rejected\n2. Add to `default_filters` list\n3. Add tests in `tests/test_search.py::TestFilters`\n\n## Current State\n\nAll 86 tests pass. peek_npts=16,\n)\npge.fit(X, Y)\n\n# Get results\nparetos = pge.get_final_paretos()\nbest = pge.get_best_model()\nprint(best.pretty_expr())\n```\n\n## Test Commands\n\n```bash\n# All tests\npython -m
